Processor Interface** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java:34)\\n- Generic interface with type parameters: `<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- Allows transformation of both keys and values\\n- Methods: `init(ProcessorContext)`, `process(Record)`, `close()`\\n- Used for key-changing operations (map, flatMap)\\n\\n**2. FixedKeyProcessor Interface** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java:33)\\n- Generic interface with type parameters: `<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- Restricts key transformation; output keys match input keys\\n- Methods: `init(FixedKeyProcessorContext)`, `process(FixedKeyRecord)`, `close()`\\n- Used for value-only transformations (filter, mapValues, flatMapValues, peek)\\n\\n**3. ProcessorSupplier Interface** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java)\\n- Factory pattern interface for creating Processor instances\\n- Allows custom initialization and reuse of Processor objects\\n- Returns new Processor instances via `get()` method\\n\\n**4. FixedKeyProcessorSupplier Interface** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java)\\n- Factory pattern interface for creating FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- Similar to ProcessorSupplier but for FixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n### Bridge Mechanism: process() and processValues() Methods\\n\\nThe DSL provides explicit bridge methods to the Processor API:\\n\\n**process() Method** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KStream.java:1550-1564)\\n- Accepts a `ProcessorSupplier<K, V, KOut, VOut>`\\n- Allows custom Processor implementation with full control\\n- Supports key-changing operations with potential repartitioning\\n- Use case: Custom state store management, complex transformations\\n\\n**processValues() Method** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/KStream.java:1580-1594)\\n- Accepts a `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, VOut>`\\n- Restricts to FixedKeyProcessor, preserving key co-location\\n- No repartitioning needed; efficient for value-only operations\\n- Use case: Custom state store management without key changes\\n\\n### Architecture Pattern\\n\\nThe DSL-to-Processor API migration follows a consistent pattern:\\n\\n1. **DSL Method** (e.g., `KStream.map()`) defines the public API\\n2. **Implementation Class** (e.g., `KStreamImpl.map()`) orchestrates the operation\\n3. **Adapter Class** (e.g., `KStreamMap`) implements `ProcessorSupplier` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier`\\n4. **Processor Class** (inner class) extends `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` and implements `process(Record)`\\n5. **Context Usage** The processor uses `context().forward()` to emit records downstream\\n\\nThis design allows teams migrating to the Processor API to:\\n- Understand how DSL operations work internally\\n- Implement custom processors with state store access\\n- Maintain similar semantics to DSL operations\\n- Access ProcessorContext features (scheduling, punctuation, state stores)\\n\\n### Key Implementation Files for Migration Reference\\n\\n- **DSL Interfaces**: KStream.java, KTable.java define all high-level operations\\n- **DSL Implementations**: KStreamImpl.java orchestrates DSL operations\\n- **Adapter Classes**: KStreamMap.java, KStreamFilter.java, etc., show how to adapt DSL operations to Processor API\\n- **Processor API Core**: Processor.java, FixedKeyProcessor.java define the low-level abstraction\\n- **Context Interfaces**: ProcessorContext.java, FixedKeyProcessorContext.java provide state store and runtime access\\n- **Record Types**: Record.java, FixedKeyRecord.java define the data flow between efficient for value-only operations\\n- Use case: Custom state store management without key changes\\n\\n### Architecture Pattern\\n\\nThe DSL-to-Processor API migration follows a consistent pattern:\\n\\n1. **DSL Method** (e.g., `KStream.map()`) defines the public API\\n2. **Implementation Class** (e.g., `KStreamImpl.map()`) orchestrates the operation\\n3. **Adapter Class** (e.g., `KStreamMap`) implements `ProcessorSupplier` or `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier`\\n4. **Processor Class** (inner class) extends `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor` and implements `process(Record)`\\n5. **Context Usage** The processor uses `context().forward()` to emit records downstream\\n\\nThis design allows teams migrating to the Processor API to:\\n- Understand how DSL operations work internally\\n- Implement custom processors with state store access\\n- Maintain similar semantics to DSL operations\\n- Access ProcessorContext features (scheduling, punctuation, state stores)\\n\\n### Key Implementation Files for Migration Reference\\n\\n- **DSL Interfaces**: KStream.java, KTable.java define all high-level operations\\n- **DSL Implementations**: KStreamImpl.java orchestrates DSL operations\\n- **Adapter Classes**: KStreamMap.java, KStreamFilter.java, etc., show how to adapt DSL operations to Processor API\\n- **Processor API Core**: Processor.java, FixedKeyProcessor.java define the low-level abstraction\\n- **Context Interfaces**: ProcessorContext.java, FixedKeyProcessorContext.java provide state store and runtime access\\n- **Record Types**: Record.java, FixedKeyRecord.java define the data flow between processors\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
